***послать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a> (362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*posъlati</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посылать.html>посыла́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to dispatch</li>
<li>to swear <i>(at someone)</i>, to tell someone to get lost</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отослать.html>отосла́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otoslátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послевоенный.html>послевое́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslevojénnyj</span>)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>е́н<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

Зализняка — 1*a.

***последний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дний</a> (152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*slědъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sleydʰ-</i> whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slide</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slither</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslédnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>last, latest, recent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v poslédneje vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">of late</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za poslédneje vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">recently</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мода.html>мо́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédnjaja</b> móda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the latest fashion</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>final, ultimate, definitive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дний</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédnij</b> srok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deadline</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédneje</b> slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the last word</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>latter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worst
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дний</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédnij</b> sort</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the worst kind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédneje</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the worst solution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́дняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poslédnjaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prostitute</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Due to negative connotations, sometimes replaced with the euphemism <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крайний.html>кра́йний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krájnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in modern colloquial usage.</li></ul>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:продолжатель.html>продолжа́тель</a>; <i>частичн.:</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторонник.html>сторо́нник</a>, эпигон</li>
</ol>

***последовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:последовать.html>после́довать</a> (2491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slédovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:последовать.html>после́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to follow, to go after</li>
<li>to follow, to be next</li>
<li>to follow, to take after</li>
<li>to follow, to do accordingly</li>
<li>to follow, to be a consequence</li>
<li>to be obliged to</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́вица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslóvica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́вицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́вицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́виц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>proverb, saying
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́вице</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́тся</a>: "<a href = vnd.unilang:артельный.html>арте́льный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипи́т</a>".</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak v <b>poslóvice</b> govorítsja: "Artélʹnyj goršók gúšče kipít".</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">As the <b>saying</b> goes: "With a helper a thousand things are possible".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:послужить.html>послужи́ть</a> (5855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">služítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послужить.html>послужи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslužítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to serve (for some time)</li>
<li>to serve, to act, to work <i>(as)</i>, to be</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>слу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-служ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:послушаться.html>послу́шаться</a> (10379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послушать.html>послу́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poslúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послушаться.html>послу́шаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslúšatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слушаться.html>слу́шаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obey, to take (someone's) advice, to listen to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послушать.html>послу́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poslúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послушный.html>послу́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslúšnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>obedient, dutiful, amenable, agreeable <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">willing to comply with</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>слу́ш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">послы́шать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poslýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послышаться.html>послы́шаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poslýšatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышаться.html>слы́шаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be heard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:послышаться.html>послы́шалось</a></b> чьё-то <a href = vnd.unilang:пение.html>пе́ние</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vdalí <b>poslýšalosʹ</b> čʹjó-to pénije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the distance singing was heard</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be felt, to be smelled</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be misheard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:послышаться.html>послы́шалось</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tebé <b>poslýšalosʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You have misheard (me).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">послы́шать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poslýšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
